<BOS> # problem: Write a function to find the top k integers that occur most frequently from given lists of sorted and distinct integers using heap queue algorithm. <NL> def func(nums, k):<NL>    import collections<NL>    d = collections.defaultdict(int)<NL>    for row in nums:<NL>        for i in row:<NL>            d[i] += 1<NL>    temp = []<NL>    import heapq<NL>    for key, v in d.items():<NL>        if len(temp) < k:<NL>            temp.append((v, key))<NL>            if len(temp) == k:<NL>                heapq.heapify(temp)<NL>        else:<NL>            if v > temp[0][0]:<NL>                heapq.heappop(temp)<NL>                heapq.heappush(temp, (v, key))<NL>    result = []<NL>    while temp:<NL>        v, key = heapq.heappop(temp)<NL>        result.append(key)<NL>    return result <EOS>

<BOS> # problem: Write a function to find k number of pairs which consist of one element from the first array and one element from the second array. <NL> import heapq<NL>def k_smallest_pairs(nums1, nums2, k):<NL>   queue = []<NL>   def push(i, j):<NL>       if i < len(nums1) and j < len(nums2):<NL>           heapq.heappush(queue, [nums1[i] + nums2[j], i, j])<NL>   push(0, 0)<NL>   pairs = []<NL>   while queue and len(pairs) < k:<NL>       _, i, j = heapq.heappop(queue)<NL>       pairs.append([nums1[i], nums2[j]])<NL>       push(i, j + 1)<NL>       if j == 0:<NL>           push(i + 1, 0)<NL>   return pairs <EOS>
